 Sixth seed Raunich defeated third seed Federer 6-3, 6-7, 4-6, 7-5, 6-3 in a marathon match
 rounich final main 2013 ke champion or duusare variya britain ke endi mare or 10wein variya check ganraajya ke thomas bardich ke bich hone vaale duusare semifinal ke vijeta se bhidenge

 rounich ne iske saath hi 2014 wimbledon semifinal main federer ke haathon mili haar kaa badla bhi chuktaa kar diya

 Federer, who won his last Grand Slam as Wimbledon in 2012, also underwent injury treatment during the fifth and deciding set when he fell on the court and suffered injuries to his right thigh and left knee
 federer se nau saal chote raonich ne paanchaven set kii shuruyaat main hi federer kii sarvice todakar 3-1 kii badhat banaai jabaki switzraland ke khilaadi ko chathe game main bhi do brake point bachaane pade
 The Canadian player, however, remained patient and won the match when Federer hit him out of the forehand court
 federer ko is tarah wimbledon semifinal main pehali baar haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa

 ) The flood situation has become catastrophic due to increase in the water level of many rivers in the northeastern states
 akele meghalaya main 75,000 log beghar ho gaye hai
 Army units have intensified relief and rescue operations
 pashchimi gaaro hills jile ke ayukta praveen bakshi ne ieenes ko bataaya ki brahmaputra or jingiram nadiyon main aae ufaan se 15,000 se zyada makaan dub gaye hai
 One of the major rivers of the Garo Hills of Meghalaya, Jingiram, has breached its main embankment, and its water has been filled in the lower areas
 abhi tak haalanki kisi kii maut kii khabar nahin he
 The district administration has demanded boats to evacuate the stranded people in the flood-affected area and has sought the help of civil defense and home guards
 bakshi ke mutabik beghar hue logon ko tehraane ke liye 15 shivi lagaae gaye hai
 Meanwhile, in Delhi, Army spokesperson Virender Singh said that the situation in Bihar and Assam, Arunachal Pradesh, has become terrible due to the Brahmaputra and its tributaries
 badhgrast ilaakon main kul 122 raahat evam bachaav dal tainaat kiye gaye hai
 According to Singh, relief operations are on in Sonitpur, Kamarup, Barpeta, Tinsukia, Sivasagar, Jorhat, Dhemaji, Baksa, Nalbari and Darang areas in Assam and Changlang in Arunachal Pradesh
 unhone bataaya ki hajaaron fanse logon bachaane ke liye sena kii timen 122 naavon or bahari injanon tathaa 540 jivan rakshak jacketon kaa istemaal kar rahi hai
 The comments ab tak lagbhag 3,500 logon ko bachaaya gaya he, jabaki sau se adhik ghayalon ko chikitsa sahaayta di gai he
 The district administration has distributed around 3,000 kg ration besides 180 packets of food among the people stranded in the floods
 singh ne bataaya ki raahat kaary main helicopteron kaa upyog bhi kiya ja rahaa he
 "military survey teams are identifying the affected areas with the help of local administration to provide immediate relief to the people," he said
 " Commissioner of West Garo Hills district, Pravin Bakshi told IANS that more than 15,000 houses were submerged by the floods in the Brahmaputra and Jingiram rivers
 meghalaya ke gaaro hills kii pramukh nadiyon main se ek jingiram ke mukhya tatbandh main daraar aa jane kii vajah se iskaa pani nichle ilaakon main bhar gaya he
 However, no death has been reported yet
 jila prashasan ne badhgrast kshetra main fanse hue logon ko nikaalane ke liye naavon kii maang kii he tathaa civil dephence or homeguard kii madad maangi he
 According to Bakshi, 15 camps have been set up to accommodate the homeless
 udhar, dilli main, sena ke pravaktaa virendra singh ne kaha ki assam or arunachal pradesh main brahmaputra or uski sahaayak nadiyon main ufaan aane se sthiti bhayaavah ho gai he
 a total of 122 relief and rescue teams have been deployed in the flood-affected areas
 singh ke anusaar, assam main sonitpur, kamrup, barpeta, tinsukiya, shivsagar, jorhat, dhemaji, baksaa, nalbadi or darang ilaakon tathaa arunachal pradesh ke changlang main raahat abhiyaan jari he
 He said that army teams are using 122 boats and external locomotives and 540 life-saving jackets to rescue thousands of stranded people
